<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grippe</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">gripper</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:seize.html>seize</a>, snatch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*grīpan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grīpaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreyb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grab.html>grab</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:grasp.html>grasp</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a> (42219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grieve.html>grieve</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">greven</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">grever</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gravō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:burden.html>burden</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Developed <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 13th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>Causing <a href = vnd.unilang:grief.html>grief</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pain.html>pain</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sorrow.html>sorrow</a>.
<ul><li><b>1883</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Louis_Stevenson" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Louis Stevenson"><a href = vnd.unilang:robert.html>Robert</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Stevenson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Treasure_Island" class="extiw" title="w:Treasure Island"><a href = vnd.unilang:treasure.html>Treasure</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:island.html>Island</a></a></i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>As</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>captain</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:his.html>his</a> wounds <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grievous.html>grievous</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:indeed.html>indeed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dangerous.html>dangerous</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:serious.html>Serious</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:grave.html>grave</a>, dire <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dangerous.html>dangerous</a>.</li></ol>

***grof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grof.html>grof</a> (4168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grof.html>grof</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:grof.html>grof</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grubaz</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a> (727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gront</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:grunt.html>grunt</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grunduz</i>.
</p>
